#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Millennium Dawn Original System Access
#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Interest Policy Check
MDACCESS_CALC_zero_interest_policy = {
	#Economic change
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_bubble_burst
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { var = interest_rate value = 2 }
	} else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_large_boned
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecosoc1
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecosoc2
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecosoc3		#Might be removed in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecolibsyn1		#Might be removed in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecolibsyn2		#Might be removed in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecolibsyn3		#Might be removed in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecolibsyn4		#Might be removed in near future
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { var = interest_rate value = 3 }
	} else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocap1
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocap2
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocap3		#Might be removed and subtract more value in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocapcor1		#Might be removed and subtract more value in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocapcor2		#Might be removed and subtract more value in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocapcor3		#Might be removed and subtract more value in near future
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_ecocapcor4		#Might be removed and subtract more value in near future
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { var = interest_rate value = 5 }
	} else_if = {
		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_REMOVE_BUBBLE_BURST		#For Decision Test
		}
		add_to_variable = { var = interest_rate value = 10 }	#For Decision Test
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_REMOVE_BUBBLE_BURST			#For Decision Test
	}
	#Disaster Change
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311_tier3
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr
			#	has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_nra
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr_nra
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { var = interest_rate value = 3 }
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = interest_rate
		min = 0.8
		max = 50
	}
	#update_AI_NO_WANT_DEBT = yes
}

#Base Debt Change Check (Compare to the Debt Before Has Been Changed)
MDACCESS_CALC_check_interest_change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = check_point_debt value = debt compare = not_equals }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EXTERNAL_DEBT_CHANGE }
				#check_variable = { var = check_point_interest_rate value = 0.8 compare = not_equals }
			}
			MDACCESS_CALC_zero_interest_policy = yes
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EXTERNAL_DEBT_CHANGE	#To Avoid 0.8% Interest by mdmosjap Additional Event
			}
			set_variable = { interest_rate = check_point_interest_rate }
			clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EXTERNAL_DEBT_CHANGE
		}
	#	calculate_debt_rate = yes
		set_variable = { check_point_debt = debt }
		#set_variable = { check_point_interest_rate = interest_rate }
		
	}
	
	#ingame_update_setup = yes
}

#CALCULATE Increase Tax Rate by 1
MDACCESS_CALC_mdmosjap_increase_tax_rate_1 = {
	#remove_tax_cost = yes
	add_to_variable = { tax_rate = 1 }
	#set_tax_cost = yes
	calculate_tax_gain = yes
	update_military_rate = yes
	#ingame_calculate_size_modifier = yes
	calculate_resource_sale_rate = yes
	set_variable = { law_attitude = 0 } #index for taxes in #_law_change_attitude arrays
	set_variable = { law_change = 1 } #-1 decrease, 1 for increase
	law_attitude_change = yes
}

#CALCULATE Decrease Tax Rate by 1
MDACCESS_CALC_mdmosjap_decrease_tax_rate_1 = {
	#remove_tax_cost = yes
	subtract_from_variable = { tax_rate = 1 }
	#set_tax_cost = yes
	calculate_tax_gain = yes
	update_military_rate = yes
	#ingame_calculate_size_modifier = yes
	calculate_resource_sale_rate = yes
	set_variable = { law_attitude = 0 } #index for taxes in #_law_change_attitude arrays
	set_variable = { law_change = -1 } #-1 decrease, 1 for increase
	law_attitude_change = yes
}

MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_increase_population_tax_rate_1 = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_increase_population_tax_rate_1_TT
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_population_tax_rate_supposed = 1 }
		MDACCESS_CALC_mdmosjap_increase_population_tax_rate = yes
		clear_variable = mdmosjap_var_population_tax_rate_supposed
	}
}

		#set_tax_cost = yes
	#	calculate_tax_gain = yes
	#	update_military_rate = yes

	#	set_variable = { law_change = 1 } #-1 decrease, 1 for increase
	#	law_attitude_change = yes
	}
}

#CALCULATE Decrease Corporate Tax Rate by 1
MDACCESS_CALC_mdmosjap_decrease_corporate_tax_rate = {
	hidden_effect = {
		#remove_tax_cost = yes
		subtract_from_variable = { corporate_tax_rate = mdmosjap_var_corporate_tax_rate_supposed }
		#set_tax_cost = yes
	#	calculate_tax_gain = yes
	#	update_military_rate = yes
	#	ingame_calculate_size_modifier = yes
	#	calculate_resource_sale_rate = yes
	#	set_variable = { law_attitude = 0 } #index for taxes in #_law_change_attitude arrays
	#	set_variable = { law_change = -1 } #-1 decrease, 1 for increase
	#	law_attitude_change = yes
	}
}

#Call Influence (Supposed to use it with scope. E.g. when you call Vietnam's value, use VIE before this.)
MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_callvalue_FROM_influence_with_CHI = {
	for_loop_effect = {																			#Start Google Search
		end = influence_array^num																#When we found what we want at num, then stop searching
		value = v																				#We don't know where is it contained that, but we knew it contains what we want
		if = {																					#
			limit = {																			#
				check_variable = { influence_array^v = CHI }									#We wanna call PRC. Call depot num where PRC contained
			}																					#
			set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_call_influence_CHI = influence_array_val^v }		#Load and copy PRC's value, then paste it to variable
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {																			#Start Google Search
		end = influence_array^num																#When we found what we want at num, then stop searching
		value = v																				#We don't know where is it contained that, but we knew it contains what we want
		if = {																					#
			limit = {																			#
				check_variable = { influence_array^v = FROM }									#We wanna call FROM. Call depot num where FROM contained (e.g. Japan calls it, FROM = JAP )
			}																					#
			set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_call_influence_FROM = influence_array_val^v }		#Load and copy FROM's value, then paste it to variable
		}
	}
}

#Clear Called Influence (Supposed to use it with scope. E.g. when you call Vietnam's value, use VIE before this.)
MDACCESS_ACT_mdmosjap_clearvalue_FROM_influence_with_CHI = {
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_call_influence_CHI
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_call_influence_FROM
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_01_from_party_pop_array_0_TT
	add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.001 } 
	hidden_effect = { add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^0 = 0.001 } recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
}

#Ruler Party Popularity: add_01
mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_01 = {
	if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_0_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_3_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_4_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_5_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_6_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_7_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_8_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_9_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_10_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_11_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 12 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_12_var_01 = yes }
	else_if = { limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } } mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_13_var_01 = yes }

#Percentage Calculation
DO_MATH_MDMOSJAP_CONCON_LEFTMOVE = {
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightCon = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftCon }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightCon = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightCon = -1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightCon }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONCON_MAXLIMIT = yes
}

DO_MATH_MDMOSJAP_CONCON_RIGHTMOVE = {
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftCon = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftCon = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftCon = -1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftCon = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftCon }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONCON_MAXLIMIT = yes
}

#Max Limit Check
CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONCON_MAXLIMIT = {
	clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftCon max = 100 min = 0 }
	clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon max = 100 min = 0 }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_GUI_CONBAR_FRAMES = yes
}

#Frame Calculation
CALC_MDMOSJAP_GUI_CONBAR_FRAMES = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon > 0 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_temp_RightCon = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightCon }
		divide_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_temp_RightCon = 100 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_temp_RightCon = 21 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ConBarFrame = mdmosjap_JAP_var_temp_RightCon }
		round_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ConBarFrame
		clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ConBarFrame max = 21 min = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ConBarFrame = 1 }
	}
}

#Radicalism Tick
decay_mdmosjap_conrad_left = {
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftRadDecayed = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = -0.2 }	#Base Decay
	
	if = {
		#JAP has SASPL idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_weak
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_middle
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_strong
				}
				NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_sealds }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.1 }
	} else_if = {
		#JAP has SEALDs idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_weak }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_middle }
					NOT = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_saspl_strong }
				}
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_sealds
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.2 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP's Leader has Cyber Left Wings idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has Lehman Shock idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_lehman_shock
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_lehman_shock_recovery
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.3 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has 3.11 idea but after the Fukushima Disaster
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311_tier2
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.3 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has 3.11 idea but having established the Reconstruction Authority
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311_tier3
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.2 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has Memory of 3.11 idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr_nra
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftRadDecayed = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDecay }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_LeftRadDecayed }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONRAD_MAXLIMIT = yes
}
decay_mdmosjap_conrad_right = {
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightRadDecayed = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = -0.2 }	#Base Decay
	
	if = {
		#JAP has Shin Rachi-giren idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_abductionleague
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP's Leader has WGIP idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = wgip
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP's Leader has Cyber Right Wings idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has Lehman Shock idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_lehman_shock
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_lehman_shock_recovery
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.3 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has 3.11 idea but after the Fukushima Disaster
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311_tier2
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.3 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has 3.11 idea but having established the Reconstruction Authority
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_311_tier3
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.2 }
	}
	if = {
		#JAP has Memory of 3.11 idea
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_aftermath_of_311_ndr_nra
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay = 0.1 }
	}
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightRadDecayed = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDecay }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_RightRadDecayed }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONRAD_MAXLIMIT = yes
}

#Max Limit Check
CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONRAD_MAXLIMIT = {
	clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad max = 100.0 min = 0.0 }
	clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad max = 100.0 min = 0.0 }
	
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_GUI_RADICON_FRAMES = yes
	CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONRAD_EFFECT = yes
}

#Radicalism Effects
CALC_MDMOSJAP_CONRAD_EFFECT = {
	#Stability Calculation from Radicalness
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablity = -0.002 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablity = -0.002 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityThreshold = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityThreshold = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad }
	subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityThreshold = 25 }
	subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityThreshold = 25 }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablity = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityThreshold }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablity = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityThreshold }
	
	#For Tooltips (Yes, I wrote this FOR JUST TOOLTIPS)
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityText = mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityThreshold }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityText = mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityThreshold }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadDestabiliablityText = -0.2 }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadDestabiliablityText = -0.2 }
}

#Frame Calculation
CALC_MDMOSJAP_GUI_RADICON_FRAMES = {
	
	#Left Icon 00
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad > 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconLowFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconLowFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Left Icon 25
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad > 25 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconMidFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconMidFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Left Icon 50
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad > 50 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconHighFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconHighFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Left Icon 75
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRad > 75 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconExtremeFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_LeftRadIconExtremeFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Right Icon 00
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad > 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconLowFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconLowFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Right Icon 25
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad > 25 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconMidFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconMidFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Right Icon 50
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad > 50 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconHighFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconHighFrame = 1 }
	}
	
	#Right Icon 75
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRad > 75 }
		}
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconExtremeFrame = 2 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_RightRadIconExtremeFrame = 1 }
	}
}

#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Mutual Defence Among East Asia
#--------------------------------------------------------------
calc_mdmosjap_apda_member = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 = 0 }
	}
	#if = {
	#	limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 } }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 = 0 }
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count_desc } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count_desc = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_research_speed_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_research_speed_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_encryption_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_encryption_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = 0 }
	}
	#if = {
	#	limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_power } }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_power = 0 }
	#}
}

recalc_mdmosjap_apda_member = {
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 = 1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count_desc = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify0 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 = -0.001 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify1 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 = 0.001 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_research_speed_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify2 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 = 0.020 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_encryption_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify3 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 = 0.020 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify4 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 = 0.020 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify5 = 0 }
	
	#add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_count }
	#multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 = 1 }
	#set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_power = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 }
	#set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_modify6 = 0 }
}

update_mdmosjap_apda_for_members = {
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_apda_MEMBER }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_research_speed_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_research_speed_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_encryption_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_encryption_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_power = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_member_effect_decryption_power }
	}
}

calc_mdmosjap_apda_altecosupports = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_count } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_count = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_sendereffect_consumer_goods_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_sendereffect_consumer_goods_factor = 0 }
	}
}

recalc_mdmosjap_apda_altecosupports = {
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify = 0.005 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_sendereffect_consumer_goods_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_altecosupports_modify = 0 }
}

calc_mdmosjap_apda_jointmaneuvers = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_count } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_count = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_sendereffect_training_time_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_sendereffect_training_time_factor = 0 }
	}
}

recalc_mdmosjap_apda_jointmaneuvers = {
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify = 0.010 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_sendereffect_training_time_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_apda_jointmaneuvers_modify = 0 }
}

		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify1 = 0 }

		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify5 = 0 }
	}
	#if = {
	#	limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 } }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 = 0 }
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count_desc } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count_desc = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_research_speed_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_research_speed_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_encryption_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_encryption_factor = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_factor = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = 0 }
	}
	#if = {
	#	limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_power } }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_power = 0 }
	#}
}

recalc_mdmosjap_anticcp_member = {
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify0 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify0 = 1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count_desc = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify0 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify0 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify1 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify1 = -0.001 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify1 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify2 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify2 = 0.001 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_research_speed_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify2 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify2 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify3 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify3 = 0.020 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_encryption_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify3 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify3 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify4 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify4 = 0.020 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify4 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify4 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify5 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify5 = 0.050 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify5 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify5 = 0 }
	
	#add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_count }
	#multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 = 1 }
	#set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_power = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 }
	#set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_modify6 = 0 }
}

update_mdmosjap_anticcp_for_members = {
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ANTICCP_MEMBER }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_consumer_goods_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_research_speed_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_research_speed_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_encryption_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_encryption_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_factor = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_factor }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_intelligence_agency_defense }
	#	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_power = JAP.mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_member_effect_decryption_power }
	}
}

calc_mdmosjap_anticcp_sanction = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_count } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_count = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_CHI_effect_consumer_goods_factor } }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_CHI_effect_consumer_goods_factor = 0 }
	}
}

recalc_mdmosjap_anticcp_sanction = {
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 = 0.025 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_CHI_effect_consumer_goods_factor = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify1 = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_count }
	multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 = -0.025 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_CHI_effect_industrial_capacity_factory = mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_sanction_modify2 = 0 }
}

		increase_mdmosjap_acceptedrefugees_rng = yes
		add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_refugeepop_TIB = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_addrefugees_rng }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_TIB = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_refugeepop_TIB }
		clamp_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_TIB max = mdmosjap_JAP_var_refugeepop_TIB_MAX min = 0 }
	#	clear_temp_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_temp_var_addrefugees_rng

increase_mdmosjap_refugeeinfluence = {
	ROOT = {
		#Copied and arranged from spread_influence 
		add_to_variable = { influence_gain = 10 }
		for_loop_effect = {				
			end = influence_array^num
			value = v
				if = {
				limit = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^v = FROM }
				}
				add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
				set_country_flag = found
			}
		}
		if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
				add_to_array = { influence_array = FROM.id }
				add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
		}
		clr_country_flag = found
		recalculate_influence = yes
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY19
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY20 }
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY20
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY21 }
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY21
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY22 }
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY22
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY23 }
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_REFERENDUM_GREAT_COALITION_INVITATION_SENT_ARRAY23
	}
}

#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Change Country Leaders
#--------------------------------------------------------------
addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI }
		hidden_effect = {
			#Add Right-wing Supports
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE }
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						}
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" } }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter
			}
			#Add Left-wing Supports
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = sayoku_supporter
			}
			#Add Moderate Supports
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LDP_COLLAPSE
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						}
						has_country_leader = { name = "Yasuo Fukuda" }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Yoshihide Suga" }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Fumio Kishida" }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Hiromu Nonaka" }
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = conservative_lib
			}
		}
	}
}

change_mdmosjap_JAP_leaders_LDP = {
	if = {
		#安倍晋三
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_SHINZO_ABE }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Shinzo Abe"
			picture = "Shinzo_Abe.dds"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = { western_conservatism emotional zealous stubborn wgip antikorea }
		}
		addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_YOSHIHIDE_SUGA
	} else_if = {
		#菅義偉
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_YOSHIHIDE_SUGA }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Yoshihide Suga"
			picture = "yoshihide_suga.dds"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = { western_conservatism rational cautious stubborn sly political_dancer mediafuror }
		}
		addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_YOSHIHIDE_SUGA
	} else_if = {
		#岸田文雄
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_FUMIO_KISHIDA }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Fumio Kishida"
			picture = "fumio_kishida.dds"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = { western_conservatism cautious humble polished likeable political_dancer }
		}
		addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_FUMIO_KISHIDA
	} else_if = {
		#石破茂
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_SHIGERU_ISHIBA }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Shigeru Ishiba"
			picture = "Shigeru_Ishiba.dds"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = { western_conservatism cautious stubborn likeable capable military_genius }
		}
		# addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_SHIGERU_ISHIBA
	} else_if = {
		#河野太郎
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_TARO_KONO }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Taro Kono"
			picture = "taro_kono.dds"
			ideology = conservatism
			traits = { western_conservatism emotional stubborn narcissist polished political_dancer }
		}
		addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_CALL_LEADER_TARO_KONO
	}
}

			picture = "hirofumi_yoshimura.dds"
			ideology = Conservative
			traits = { emerging_Conservative emotional rash polished likeable mediafuror lawyer }
		}

	} else_if = {

	}
}

#森喜朗
changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_summon_yoshiro_mori = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = communism }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Yoshiro Mori" picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds" ideology = Conservative
		#	traits = { western_conservatism emotional stubborn narcissist }
			traits = { western_conservatism }
		}
	} else = {
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Yoshiro Mori" picture = "yoshiro_mori.dds" ideology = conservatism
		#	traits = { western_conservatism emotional stubborn narcissist }
			traits = { western_conservatism }
		}
	}
	if = {	#えひめ丸チェック
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_PROGOLFER_MORI }
		add_country_leader_trait = incapable
	}
	addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_abductee_rescuer_removal = yes
	addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
}

	}

	addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes

		name = "Keishi Takami" picture = "generic_radical_left_rebel_JAP_censored.dds" ideology = anarchist_communism
		traits = { emerging_anarchist_communism permanent_revolutionary }
	}
	addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_abductee_rescuer_removal = yes
	addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = yes
}

#Trait Check ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
#Remove 'Abductee Rescuer' trait (for regime change)
addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_abductee_rescuer_removal = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer1 }
		remove_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = abductee_rescuer2 }
		remove_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
	}
}

#Add 'Abductee Rescuer' Trait after an election
addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_abductee_rescuer = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1 }
		add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer1
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2 }
		add_country_leader_trait = abductee_rescuer2
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TRAITMEMORY_ABDUCTEE_RESCUER2
	}
}

#Add 'Cyber Right Wings' Trait
addcheck_mdmosjap_JAP_zaitokukai = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ZAITOKUKAI
			has_country_leader_with_trait = western_conservatism
			NOT = { has_country_leader_with_trait = conservative_lib }
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_country_leader_trait = uyoku_supporter }
	}
}

		set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_YOSHIKI_YAMASHITA days = 1095 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {

	}
	
	#JIP

		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_KAZUMI_INAMURA
		set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_KAZUMI_INAMURA days = 1095 value = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Hitoshi Nakamura" } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_HITOSHI_NAKAYAMA
		set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_HITOSHI_NAKAYAMA days = 1095 value = 1 }
	}
	
	#Zaitokukai-JFP Lineage
	if = {

	}

		set_country_flag = { flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_TETSUOU_UOTANI days = 1095 value = 1 }
	}

#Remedy for vacancy of candidates on the SDP
changepm_mdmosjap_JAP_candidates_remedy_for_SDP = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MIZUHO_FUKUSHIMA
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_SEIJI_MATAICHI
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_KIYOMI_TSUJIMOTO
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MIZUHO_FUKUSHIMA
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_SEIJI_MATAICHI
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_KIYOMI_TSUJIMOTO
	} else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MIZUHO_FUKUSHIMA
				has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_SEIJI_MATAICHI
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_MIZUHO_FUKUSHIMA
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_RESIGNATION_COOLDOWN_SEIJI_MATAICHI
	}
}

#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Election Scripts
#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Hold Election
election_mdmosjap_JAP_hold_election = {
#	election_mdmosjap_JAP_update_next_election_date = yes
	election_mdmosjap_JAP_calc_date_of_election_relative_events = yes
	
	hidden_effect = {
		#Constitution Amendment Referendum Check
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_a_majority_by_revisionist = yes	#Revisionist holds more than 51% of popularity
					trigger_mdmosjap_has_radicalism_right_66 = yes			#More than Two-Thirds of the national people are the Radical Rightists
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.2002 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_Referendum }		#Hold Referendum Campaign 21 days before
		}
		
		#Election Event Check
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1100 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_HoldCampaign }			#Hold Election Campaign 14 days before
	#	country_event = { id = MD4_election_campaign.0 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_HoldCampaign }				#Original Event
	
		#Komeito Check
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_komeito }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.2001 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_KomeitoSupport }	#Komeito's Support to LDP 7 days before
		}
		
		#After Election Regime Check
	#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1000 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_RulingPartyCheck }		#Ruling Party Check 1 days after
	#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japanelection.1002 days = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_LDPCoalitionCheck }	#LDP Partisan Coalition Check 4 days after
	}
	hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
	set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
	
	custom_effect_tooltip = election_mdmosjap_JAP_hold_election_TT
}

#Update Next Election Date
election_mdmosjap_JAP_update_next_election_date = {
	#Prevents Disappearing of Guarantees
	every_other_country = {
		limit = { has_guaranteed = FROM }
	#	set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_GUARANTEED_JAPAN
		add_to_array = { mdmosjap_array_guaranteee_disappearing_prevention_country = FROM }
	}
	
	#Loading Current Date for the Next Election Date in the Freqency
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = democratic }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]" election_frequency = 48 elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = communism }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]" election_frequency = 48 elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = fascism }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]" election_frequency = 48 elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = neutrality }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]" election_frequency = 48 elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_government = nationalist }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]" election_frequency = 48 elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
	
	#Reload Disappeared Guarantees
#	every_other_country = {
#		limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_GUARANTEED_JAPAN }
#		give_guarantee = FROM
#		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_TEMP_GUARANTEED_JAPAN
#	}
	every_other_country = {
		limit = { is_in_array = { mdmosjap_array_guaranteee_disappearing_prevention_country = FROM } }
		give_guarantee = FROM
		clear_array = mdmosjap_array_guaranteee_disappearing_prevention_country
	}
}

#Calculate Date of Election-Relative Events
election_mdmosjap_JAP_calc_date_of_election_relative_events = {
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_HoldCampaign = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_KomeitoSupport = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_Referendum = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_RulingPartyCheck = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod }
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_LDPCoalitionCheck = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod }
	subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_HoldCampaign = 14 }
	subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_KomeitoSupport = 7 }
	subtract_from_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_Referendum = 15 }
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_RulingPartyCheck = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_LDPCoalitionCheck = 4 }
}

#Clear Date of Election-Relative Events
election_mdmosjap_JAP_clear_date_of_election_relative_events = {
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionPeriod
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_HoldCampaign
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_KomeitoSupport
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_Referendum
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_RulingPartyCheck
	clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_ElectionEvent_LDPCoalitionCheck
	clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_LOWER_ELECTION
}

#--------------------------------------------------------------
#Capitulation Scripts
#--------------------------------------------------------------
capitulation_mdmosjap_CHI = {
	#THE SCRIPT MUST BE OCCURED BY "CHI" TAG
	
	#Making Peace with CHI Faction excepts CHI
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_war = yes	
			NOT = { tag = CHI }
			has_capitulated = no
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = CHI
				is_subject_of = CHI
				is_puppet_of = CHI
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = PREV
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_member
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_apda_member
					is_in_faction_with = TAI
				}
			}
			white_peace = PREV	#イベントで休戦できるか選択できるようにすること
		}
	}
	
	#Free All Puppets
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = CHI
				is_puppet_of = CHI
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
		}
	}
	
	#Remove from Faction / Dissolve Faction
	if = {
		limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		dismantle_faction = yes
	} else_if = {
		limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
		leave_faction = yes
	}
	
	#Transfer ETK core and claimed states
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CHI
				is_controlled_by = CHI
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = ETK
				is_claimed_by = ETK
			}
			country_exists = ETK
			ETK = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
		}
		ETK = { transfer_state = PREV }
	}
	#Transfer TIB core and claimed states
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CHI
				is_controlled_by = CHI
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = TIB
				is_claimed_by = TIB
			}
			country_exists = TIB
			TIB = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
			OR = {		#Aksai Chin - Arunachal Pradesh Check
				NOT = { is_core_of = RAJ }
				AND = {
					is_core_of = RAJ
					NOT = { is_owned_by = RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		TIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
	}
	#Transfer Aksai Chin to RAJ if they are in war
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CHI
				is_controlled_by = CHI
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = RAJ
				is_claimed_by = RAJ
			}
			country_exists = RAJ
			RAJ = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
		}
		RAJ = { transfer_state = PREV }
	}
	#Transfer TAI core and claimed states
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = CHI
				is_controlled_by = CHI
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = TAI
				is_claimed_by = TAI
			}
			country_exists = TAI
			TAI = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
			OR = {		#Aksai Chin - Arunachal Pradesh Check
				NOT = { is_core_of = RAJ }
				AND = {
					is_core_of = RAJ
					NOT = { is_owned_by = RAJ }
				}
			}
		}
		TAI = { transfer_state = PREV }
	}
	#Transfer rest of state to Expandist Japan when they have a purpose
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_controlled_by = CHI
			NOT = { is_core_of = CHI }
			NOT = { is_claimed_by = CHI }
			country_exists = JAP
			JAP = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge1
					has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_refugees_revenge2
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
			}
		}
		JAP = { transfer_state = PREV }
	}
	
	#Remove SCO Ideas from the World
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_idea = sco_member }
		remove_ideas = sco_member
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_idea = sco_observer }
		remove_ideas = sco_observer
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_idea = sco_member_econ }
		remove_ideas = sco_member_econ
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_idea = sco_member_pol }
		remove_ideas = sco_member_pol
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = { has_idea = sco_member_mil }
		remove_ideas = sco_member_mil
	}
	
	#Remove CHI core-claims if CHI doesn't exist
#	every_state = {
#		limit = {
#		#	NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
#			is_core_of = CHI
#		}
#		remove_core_of = CHI	#イベントでCHIを消去するかどうか選択できるようにするべき？
#	}
#	every_state = {
#		limit = {
#		#	NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
#			is_claimed_by = CHI
#		}
#		remove_claim_by = CHI	#イベントでCHIを消去するかどうか選択できるようにするべき？
#	}
}

#--------------------------------------------------------------
#The Crisis of Autumn Equinox Calculation
#--------------------------------------------------------------
calc_mdmosjap_kato_rebellion_epilogue_kono_ending_crisis_result = {
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_L_absolute = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_R_absolute = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = 0 }
	if = {	#I am not good at mathematics since 7th grade :(
		limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R } }
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = 0 }
	} else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L > mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R > 0 }		#ex)  4 v 2  (2)
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R = 0 }		#ex)  4 v 0  (4)
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R < 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L > 0 }	#ex)  2 v -2 (4)
						check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L = 0 }	#ex)  0 v -2 (2)
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_R_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
				multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_R_absolute = -1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_R_absolute }
			} else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L < 0 }	#ex) -1 v -2 (1)
				}
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
			}
		}
	} else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L < mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L > 0 }		#ex)  2 v 4  (2)
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L = 0 }		#ex)  0 v 4  (4)
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L < 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R > 0 }	#ex) -2 v 2  (4)
						check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R = 0 }	#ex) -2 v 0  (2)
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_L_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
				multiply_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_L_absolute = -1 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_L_absolute }
			} else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R < 0 }	#ex) -2 v -1 (1)
				}
				set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_R }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute = mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_L }
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference = mdmosjap_temp_var_shubun_kiki_point_difference_absolute }	
}
